1 1. 1. 1.  A d verse E ve nt  
A n A E (als o r eferre d t o as a n a d vers e e x perie nce) is a n y u nt o w ar d me dic al occ urre nce ass ociat e d 
wit h t he use of a dr u g i n h u ma ns, w het her or n ot c o nsi dere d dr u g relate d. A n A E ca n t heref ore

or disease te m p orall y ass ociate d wit h t he use of a dr u g, w het her or n ot c o nsi dere d 
relate d t o t he dr u g. 
  A n y n e w di seas e or e x acer bati o n of a n e xisti n g disease (a w ors e ni n g i n t he c haracter, 
fre q ue n c y, or se v erit y of a k n o w n c o n diti o n).

baseli ne.  
  A n y d eteri or ati o n i n a la b orat or y val ue or ot h er cli nical test (e g, E C G, X -ra y) t hat is 
ass ociate d wit h s y m pt o ms or lea ds t o a c h a n ge i n st u d y treat me nt or c o nc o mita nt 
treat me nt or disc o nti n uati o n fr o m st u d y treat me nt. 
  A d verse e ve nts t hat are relate d t o a pr ot oc ol -ma n date d i nter ve nti o n, i ncl u di n g t h os e 
t hat occ ur pri or t o assi g n me nt of st u d y treat me nt ( e g, s cree ni n g i n vasi ve pr oce d ures 
s uc h as bi o psies).

dr u g) a n d fr o m a n y r o ute of a d mi nistrati o n, f or m ulati o n, or d ose, i ncl u di n g a n o ver d ose.
